## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Defined: Create Application
    Defined --> Syncing: Auto Sync Triggered
    Syncing --> Synced: Deployment Success
    Synced --> OutOfSync: Configuration Drift
    OutOfSync --> Syncing: Self Heal Enabled
    Synced --> Pruning: Resources Removed
    Pruning --> Synced: Prune Complete
    Synced --> [*]: Delete Application
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Application {
        +String apiVersion
        +String kind
        +Metadata metadata
        +Spec spec
    }
    class Metadata {
        +String name
    }
    class Spec {
        +Destination destination
        +Source source
        +Array sources
        +String project
        +SyncPolicy syncPolicy
    }
    class Destination {
        +String name
        +String namespace
        +String server
    }
    class Source {
        +String repoURL
        +String chart
        +String targetRevision
        +Helm helm
    }
    class Helm {
        +Array valueFiles
        +Array parameters
    }
    class SyncPolicy {
        +Automated automated
    }
    class Automated {
        +Boolean prune
        +Boolean selfHeal
    }
    
    Application --> Metadata
    Application --> Spec
    Spec --> Destination
    Spec --> Source
    Spec --> SyncPolicy
    Source --> Helm
    SyncPolicy --> Automated
```
